 Who was Dadasaheb Phalke Dada Saheb Phalke, born on 30 April 1870 in a Marathi family, studied from Nashik
 dada sahib phalke kaa puraa naam dhundiraj govind phalke tha

 in awords kii shuruyaat saal 1969 main hui thi
 Dada Saheb Phalke is called the father of Indian cinema

 On Wednesday, about a dozen councilors of the Aam Aadmi Party filed a complaint with the Anti Corruption Bureau in Delhi
 parshadon kaa aarope he ki bijepi shasit dilli nagar nigam ne bhrashtachar kii sari simaaen tod di hai

 aam aadmi party parshad praveen kumaar ne kaha ki agar is puure maamle main sahi dhang se jaanch hoti he to maamla kai guna or bada ho saktaa he

 bijepi boli- ham khud kara rahe hai jaanchauttari dilli nagar nigam main dipti meyar yogesh verma se jab is puure maamle main sawaal poocha gaya to unka kahana he ki audit report main gadabadiyon kii jaankaree unke paas he or vah khud is puure maamle kii jaanch karvaa rahe hai or kisi bhi doshi ko bakhsha nahin jayega
 Investment management company kkr-backed Radiant Life Care will buy a majority stake in Max Healthcare, which runs a chain of hospitals
 adhigrahan ke baad banane vaali sanyukt company kaa mulya 7,242 karod rupee hoga
 The deal will take place in multiple stages, with KKR holding a majority stake in the combined entity after the deal, while Abhay Soi, promoter of Radiant Life Care, will head the joint company
 maiks healthcare ke pravartak anlajit singh pad se hat jaaenge
 The two companies said in a joint statement, 'radiant and Max Healthcare will be the largest hospital network in North India, being a joint venture
 yah rajasav ke lihaaj se bharat ke sheersh teen aspataal network main shaamil hogi
 Not only this, it will be the fourth largest hospital chain in the country based on the number of beds
 'yah adhigrahan kai charnon ke lenden ke jariye puraa hoga, jisamen dakshin africa kii aspataal runkhalaa life healthcare kii maiks healthcare main hissedari kii kharid bhi shaamil he
 49 in Max of Life Healthcare
 7 pratishat hissedari he
 As part of the deal, Max India will divest its non-healthcare business, including Max Bupa and Anatara Senior Living, which will join the wholly owned subsidiary of Max India, which has separate shares on the Bombay Stock Exchange and National Stock - will be listed separately
 jharkhand ke ranchi jile ke mander ilaake ke kanijia gaanv main kal der raat graminon ne 'dian' bataakar lathi-danda se peet kar paanch mahilaon kii hatya kar di
 Police arrested 27 people in this case
 ranchi ke police upmahanireekshak arun kumaar ne bataaya ki kal der raat rajdhani ranchi se bees kilometre dur mander ilaake main kanijia gaanv main ek dil dahala dene vaali ghatana main gaanv waalon ne 'dian' bataakar lathi-danda se peet kar 32 se 50 saal kii umr kii paanch mahilaon kii nirmam hatya kar di
 After this, their dead bodies were tied in sacks and thrown out of the village
 unhone bataaya ki police ne shuruaati jaanch ke baad nrushans hatya ke is maamle main lagbhag pachaas logon ke khilaaf hatya kii exiaar darj kii he or inamen se 27 logon ko giraftaar bhi kar liya he
 Meanwhile, Chief Minister Raghuvar Das expressed anguish over the incident, saying, 'in this age of knowledge and information, such an event shames humanity
 ' unhone samaaj se jaagane or aisi ghatnaon ko rokane ke liye logon main chetana failaane ko kaha he
 He has asked the police to take stern action against those involved in the incident
 vahiin police upmahanireekshak ne bataaya ki maare gaye logon ke shavon kaa postmortem police ne karvaa liya he or sabhi ko maare jane kaa kaaran un par lathi danda se waar hi sabit hua he
 He said that he himself is still on the scene, and a large number of police forces have been deployed throughout the area
 graminon ne andhvishwaas ke chalate sabere police ke gaanv pahunchakar laash kabje main lene kaa bhi virodh kiya or gaanv ke kabrgah main unhen dafnane kaa bhi vah virodh kar rahe hai
 Giving details of the incident, Arun Kumar said that a few days ago two-three middle-aged people died in the village due to unknown reasons, which some people said was a death due to the influence of 'witch'
 iske baad abhi do dinon pehle maari gai mahilaon main se ek ke ghar ke pados main 18 saal ke yuvak kii pilia se maut ho gai
 The Deputy Inspector General of Police said that the villagers started beating a woman living in the neighborhood of the dead youth as a witch
 pitati mahila ne chaar duusari mahilaon kaa naam liya or gaanv waalon ne unhen bhi unke gharon se nikaalkar lathi danda se peetna shuru kar diya, jisase paanchon mahilaon ne vahiin dam tod diya
 He informed that the state government and especially the Chief Minister has taken the entire incident very seriously and strict action will be taken against it
 faraar aropiyon kii police jorshor se talash kar rahi he or raat tak sabhi ko giraftaar kar liye jane kii sambhaavna he
 The comments duusari ore, rajya ke nagar vikaas mantri or ranchi ke vidhayak seepi singh ne is ghatana par gaharaa dukh prakat karte hue logon se aisi kuritiyon se dur hone kii apil kii
 He talked of running programs to bring awareness against such evils in public
 rajya mahila ayog kii adhyaksh mahua maanjhi ne bhi ghatana kii ninda kii or kaha ki vah apni team ke saath do-teen dinon main ghatnasthal kaa daura karengi or iskaa jayja lengi
 She said that such incidents are mostly done under conspiracy either due to confusion or due to the intention of grabbing the property of single women
 unhone kaha ki aisi ghatnaon kii punrariti rokane ke liye uchit mahila niti kii jarurat he
 Ranchi Deputy Inspector General of Police Arun Kumar said that in a heartbreaking incident at Kanijia village in Mandar area, twenty kilometers from the capital Ranchi, late last night, the villagers beat them with sticks and sticks as 'witch', aged between 32 and 50 Killed five women ruthlessly
 iske baad unki laashon ko bore main baandhakar gaanv se baahar phenk diya
 He said that after preliminary investigation, police have registered an FIR for murder against about fifty people in this case of brutal murder and 27 of them have been arrested
 is bich, mukhyamantri raghuvar das ne ghatana par kshobh vyakt karte hue kaha, 'gyaan or soochna ke is yug main is tarah kii ghatana se maanavtaa sharmasaar hoti he
 'he has asked the society to wake up and spread consciousness among people to prevent such incidents
 unhone police se is ghatana main shaamil logon ke khilaaf kathor karrwai karne ko kaha he
 On the other hand, Deputy Inspector General of Police said that the post mortem of the dead bodies has been done by the police and the reason for killing all is proved to be a stab with sticks
 unhone bataaya ki vah swayan abhi bhi mauka-e-vaardaat par hi hai, or puure ilaake main badi sankhya main police bal kii tainaati kii gai he
 The villagers also protested against the police taking possession of the corpse by reaching the village early in the morning due to superstition and they are also opposed to burying them in the village cemetery
 arun kumaar ne ghatana kaa vivaran dete hue bataaya ki kuch dinon pehle gaanv main do teen adhed umr ke logon kii agyaat kaarnon se maut ho gai jise kuch logon ne 'dian' ke prabhaav se hui maut bataakar logon main bhranti failaane kaa kaam kiya
 After this, an 18-year-old man died of jaundice in the neighborhood of the house of one of the women killed just two days ago
 police upmahanireekshak ne bataaya ki gaanv waalon ne mrit yuvak ke pados main rahane vaali ek mahila ko dian bataakar peetna shuru kar diya
 The beaten woman took the names of four other women and the villagers also took them out of their houses and started beating them with sticks, which caused the five women to die there itself
 unhone bataaya ki rajya sarkaar or khaskar mukhyamantri ne puri ghatana ko bahut gambhirtha se liya he or iske khilaaf sakht karrwai kii jaaegi
 The police are vigorously searching for the absconding accused and all are likely to be arrested by night
 tippaniyan On the other hand, the state's Urban Development Minister and Ranchi MLA CP Singh expressed deep sorrow over this incident and appealed to the people to get away from such malpractices

 China’s ambitious Silk Road project has been clouded by crisis
 indonesia main jahaan ek rail pariyojna ataki padi he, vahiin pakistan main aarthik gaaliara charampanthi khatre se jujh rahaa he
 This could push the shiny economic policy image of Chinese President Xi Jinping
 shi jinping ne china ko africa, asia or europe se bandargahon, railway, sadak or audyogic parkon ke jariye jodne kii 'van belt, van road' yojana ko 2013 main shuru kiya tha
 Many experts estimate that the project will cost one thousand billion dollars
 shi jinping pichley kai dashakon main china ke sabase majboot netaa ke taur par ubhare hai
 He laid great emphasis on the infrastructure sector to expand China's economic and geopolitical interests
 yahi vajah rahi ki chini congress kii pichley maheene hui ahm baithak main jinping kii vichaardhaara ko communist party ke samvidhan main jagah di gai
 After China's first Communist leader and founder Maotse Tung and former President Deng Xiaoping, Xi is the only leader whose ideas have been included in the party's constitution
 communist party kii is baithak main shi jinping kibelt and rodpariyojna kii kaaphi saraahna kii gai
 The project spans around 65 countries
 haalanki jameen halaat dekhen to is pariyojna main kai rode dikh rahe hai
 The project passes between terrorism-affected areas, dictatorial regimes and uprooted democratic countries
 iske alaava ise kai bhrasht netaaon or sthaneey logon ke virodh ke kaaran sankat kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he
 "the construction of infrastructure in such countries is quite complex," says Murray Heibert, a think tank at the Washington-based Center for Strategic and International Studies (CSIS), which has studied various such projects in Southeast Asia
